  <raw>Brain lint



How much of 2002 is left in your mind?
Another day, another month. Today it's October. Your time starts now.

Q1 Which radical Muslim cleric was formally detained by Indonesian authorities in a security crackdown after the Bali bombings?
Q2 Who won the Cunningham by-election, creating history by becoming the first Green to win a seat in the Federal Parliament's House of Representatives?
Q3 Which two senior federal politicians accompanied John Howard when he flew to Bali?
Q4 Which singer won both the ARIA best female artist and album of the year awards?
Q5 Who asked his people in a referendum if he should remain president for another seven years?
Q6 Who won the 2002 Nobel Peace Prize?
Q7 Whose blood did Northern Territory police find matched the DNA found on the T-shirt of Joanne Lees?
Q8 Two bombs exploded in Bali's nightclub district. Where in Denpasar did the third bomb explode?
Q9 Which British politician shocked the world when it was revealed he had an affair with Edwina Currie in the 1980s?
Q10 Which Aussie was sacked as artistic director of London's Royal Ballet company after completing only one year of a three-year contract?
Q11 Which federal politician told a joint government parties meeting: "I'm sure, like me, you've all picked up a surprising amount of anti-American sentiment in the community"?
1. Abu Bakar Bashir, 2. Michael Organ, 3. John Anderson and Simon Crean, 4. Kasey Chambers, 5. Saddam Hussein, 6. Jimmy Carter, 7. Bradley John Murdoch,
8. Outside the US consulate, 9. John Major, 10. Ross Stretton, 11. John Anderson.</raw>
